 THE DOSE TIMES, THE DOSE AMOUNTS (INCLUDING ALL BOLUS
 VALUES AND THE IV RATES), AND THE OBSERVATION TIMES WHICH THE
 PROGRAM READ FROM THE WORKING COPY PATIENT DATA FILE ABOVE
 WERE ALL ASSUMED TO BE "NOISY" VALUES.

 EACH DOSE TIME IS MADE "NOISY" AS FOLLOWS:
 THE FIRST DOSE TIME, WITH A TRUE VALUE OF VTRUE, WILL BE 
 CHANGED TO BE VNOISY, WHERE VNOISY = VTRUE + Ei, WHERE
 Ei ~ N(0,STDI**2), WHERE 
 STDI = C0 + C1*VTRUE + C2*VTRUE**2 + C3*VTRUE**3

 FOR SUBSEQUENT DOSE TIMES, THE NOISY DOSE TIME IS 
 DETERMINED AS FOLLOWS:
 a. SET DUR = NOMINAL DURATION BETWEEN THE PREVIOUS DOSE TIME 
    AND THE CURRENT DOSE TIME.
 b. CALC. THE NOISY DURATION, DURNOISY, AS 
    DURNOISY = DUR + Ei, Ei ~ N(0,STDI**2), WHERE 
    STDI = C0 + C1*DUR + C2*DUR**2 + C3*DUR**3
 c. ... BUT LIMIT DURNOISY TO BE .GE. .5*DUR AND .LE. 2*DUR.
 d. SET THE CURRENT NOISY DOSE TIME = PREVIOUS NOISY DOSE TIME
    + DURNOISY.

 THE SAME LOGIC APPLIES FOR OBS. TIMES. 

 NOTE THIS LOGIC --> TIMES CANNOT BE OUT OF ORDER.

 EACH IV RATE AND EACH BOLUS VALUE WHICH = 0 WILL NOT
 BE MADE NOISY. I.E., IT IS ASSUMED THAT IF A RATE OR BOLUS IS
 INTENDED TO BE 0, IT WILL BE ACHIEVED WITHOUT ERROR.
 A NON-ZERO IV OR BOLUS VALUE, WITH A TRUE VALUE OF VTRUE, 
 WILL BE CHANGED TO BE VNOISY, WHERE VNOISY = VTRUE + Ei, WHERE
 Ei ~ N(0,STDI**2), WHERE 
 STDI = C0 + C1*VTRUE + C2*VTRUE**2 + C3*VTRUE**3
